  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_79601233-86d2-4fc9-b658-ce88f989d75a'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer4983398843772548166">One look at Brawn and Becca is wondering how he’d look without his clothes. Brawn is instantly attracted to Becca but has sworn never to touch a human female. They just aren’t sturdy enough and he likes his sex a little rough. He is shocked to learn he’ll be living with her when she refuses to leave her home. He is there to represent New Species and to learn about humans s</span>
  <span id="freeText4983398843772548166" style="display:none">One look at Brawn and Becca is wondering how he’d look without his clothes. Brawn is instantly attracted to Becca but has sworn never to touch a human female. They just aren’t sturdy enough and he likes his sex a little rough. He is shocked to learn he’ll be living with her when she refuses to leave her home. He is there to represent New Species and to learn about humans so maybe this will be a good educational experience. He just has to keep his hands off her.<br /><br />His good intentions go astray when they are kidnapped and locked together inside a cage. Brawn finds himself reliving a nightmare when he is once again subjected to breeding experiments at the hands of New Species’ enemies. They will use Becca to get what they want from him. Brawn will do everything he can to protect her but they only have each other to depend on while trying to survive.</span>

<span class='communityAnswerText'>
<span class="expandableContainer"><span class="truncatedContent">Since I bing-read all the books, I don't remember in which they explain it, but they do mention a few times throughout the series, that since everythi<a class="jsShow showAction" href="#">…more</a></span><span class="fullContent">Since I bing-read all the books, I don't remember in which they explain it, but they do mention a few times throughout the series, that since everything about species is dominant, even their genes, then their male gene dominates and therefore male species and human females only make boys.<br /><br />****SPOILER ALERT**** (Kind of)<br /><br />In this theory, should they get the female species reproductive functions to work, and they mate with human males, then they should be able to make girls.<a class="jsHide hideAction" href="#">(less)</a></span></span>
</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1210937249" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer3282534275846704933"><b> 4 Baby's mama drama Stars</b><br/><br/><b>*Spoilers*</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/iSWA5Xd5zU8hT_zpsexwuhzut.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1424976179ra/13826185.gif' alt=' photo iSWA5Xd5zU8hT_zpsexwuhzut.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><br/><b>“I like directness too. I did take it wrong at first and mentally agreed it would be a tight fit. You’re small. For a second, as I admired your bent form, I forgot why I’d never touch a human female and I growled in appreciation. My kind do that when we’re aroused. You have a nice form.” </b><br/><br/>Brawn is the 5th book in the New Species Series and it is chock full of dramatic goodness. Brawn is the new member of the task force team that becca's father leads. He has</span>
  <span id="freeText3282534275846704933" style="display:none"><b> 4 Baby's mama drama Stars</b><br><br><b>*Spoilers*</b><br><br><a href="http://s327.photobucket.com/user/jessica_hatfield1/media/iSWA5Xd5zU8hT_zpsexwuhzut.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<span id="freeTextContainer4564606530743723920">2.5/5<br/><br/>This was a huge disappointment. This book had high potential to be a 4 or even 5 stars read for me, but unfortunately it fell far short of my expectations. The story started off promising but somewhere around halfway through the third quarter, it started to go off track, and finally ended up being only a mediocre read for me.<br/><br/>Despite the fact that I found the story itself was fun, the plot was interesting and Brawn was so adorable, there were still so many things that didn't work for me in t</span>
  <span id="freeText4564606530743723920" style="display:none">2.5/5<br /><br />This was a huge disappointment. This book had high potential to be a 4 or even 5 stars read for me, but unfortunately it fell far short of my expectations. The story started off promising but somewhere around halfway through the third quarter, it started to go off track, and finally ended up being only a mediocre read for me.<br /><br />Despite the fact that I found the story itself was fun, the plot was interesting and Brawn was so adorable, there were still so many things that didn't work for me in this book. As the story went on, I became more and more frustrated with Becca and the people around her and Brawn. I wanted to pull my hair out when Becca kept trying to make a mindless decision, and she was far too stubborn about her pregnancy and the father of her child.<br /><br />The people around this couple were so annoying. Not only didn't they help make anything better, they tried to interfere with Brawn and Becca, like they didn't want him to reconcile with her. WTH! Slade and Trisha had annoyed me since I'd read their book (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1508947354?book_show_action=false" rel="nofollow noopener">Slade</a>, the second installment in New Species series) and they just showed up in this book to annoy me again! (Someone throw these two awful people out of this book please!)<br /><br />The romance between Brawn and Becca availed me nothing. The author failed to convince me that both of them had had strong feelings for each other. I didn't believe one little bit of that!<br /><br />This is the fifth installment in the series but there was still not much depth to the heroine's character, not different from the previous books. In this one, how could Becca had no close friends, no colleagues, or no relatives, except her father and her late husband's family in Europe?! It was totally unrealistic!<br /><br />However, I was satisfied with the ending. The author did a great job on this wonderful HEA.<br /><br />By the way, if it weren't for Brawn, I would give this book 2 stars. Enough said!<br /><br /><br />------------------------------<br /><br /><br />**BR with my lovely friends, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/4150124-aileene" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-nynaeve" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a>.</span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dino-Jess ✮ The Book Eating Dinosaur ✮" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dino-Jess ✮ The Book Eating Dinosaur ✮" href="/user/show/27279812-dino-jess-the-book-eating-dinosaur">Dino-Jess ✮ The Book Eating Dinosaur ✮</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781419967764" href="/book/show/17240413-brawn">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Dino-Jess ✮ The Book Eating Dinosaur ✮ by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/22911953-monty-cupcake-queen-of-bloodshed">Monty Cupcake ☠ Queen of Bloodshed ☠</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27279812-dino-jess-the-book-eating-dinosaur?shelf=vitamin-d">vitamin-d</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27279812-dino-jess-the-book-eating-dinosaur?shelf=i-need-a-cold-shower">i-need-a-cold-shower</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27279812-dino-jess-the-book-eating-dinosaur?shelf=seriously-that-cover-omg">seriously-that-cover-omg</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1463925101" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10273437975351027959"><b>This installment of the mind-crack made me mad. </b><br/> <br/>The other books in this series have all been <u>hellishly flawed</u>, but I've been able to enjoy them regardless. This one, not so much. <br/> <br/>If I could rate just the first half of this book, this would get 4 stars, easy. I found the whole kidnapping plot fascinating. Brawn and Becca's experiences while in captivity are hot, and while I don't think I would be rushing to bang my cellmate under their circumstances, the whole thing worked for me, with limited </span>
  <span id="freeText10273437975351027959" style="display:none"><b>This installment of the mind-crack made me mad. </b><br /> <br />The other books in this series have all been <u>hellishly flawed</u>, but I've been able to enjoy them regardless. This one, not so much. <br /> <br />If I could rate just the first half of this book, this would get 4 stars, easy. I found the whole kidnapping plot fascinating. Brawn and Becca's experiences while in captivity are hot, and while I don't think I would be rushing to bang my cellmate under their circumstances, the whole thing worked for me, with limited eye rolls.<br /><br /><b>Brawn is wonderful</b>. He's a stud. He has stamina for days. He knows how to please a lady. He says swoon worthy things. He's not wearing <u>ANY</u> clothes on the cover of the book. <b>Would bang</b>.<br /> <br />But around half way through this story, when they got out of the cage, everything started to go downhill.<br /> <br />Becca turns into a <b>FUCKING STUBBORN IDIOT</b> and I wanted to stab her in her stupid face. Seriously. You <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ get pregnant with a New Species baby and expect to be able to keep it a secret out in the real world?!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> Just how delusional are you? <br /><br />Her father, Tim, deserves a giant kick in the dick. How dare you do what you did to keep Brawn and Becca apart. You selfish asshole. <br /><br />The lack of communication between the characters in this is <u>atrocious</u>. The fact that Brawn and Becca need multiple people at multiple times to mediate their discussions, is fucking stupid. Why don't you two just sit down and actually <b>TALK TO EACH OTHER</b> and then maybe you would be able to see that you are both being stupid and can be together and don't need a bazillion people involved in your shit.<br /><br />Oh! And the thing that makes me the most ragey about this book is the fact that after Becca and Brawn's encounter in the cage, during Becca's check up <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Trisha tried to give Becca the morning after pill <b>WITHOUT TELLING HER</b>, effectively taking away any choice that Becca has in terms of her body. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> The justification of this in the book is absolutely <b>ludicrous</b>. A woman should <u>ALWAYS</u> have the right to choose what to do with her own body. The fact that another woman took this choice away from her, makes it even worse. <b>I loathe this part of the story with the fire of a thousand suns</b>. <br /><br />All the swoon worthy lines that Brawn says, cannot make up for the burning rage I feel about the above spoiler. It really ruined the second part of the book for me. <br /><br />The writing in this is an improvement on the previous installments, the sexy times were hot and there were noticeably fewer errors. <br /><br />I <i>will</i> keep going with this series, but I think I need a little break from it. <br /><br /><b>2</b> <i>open-your-mouth</i> <b>Stars</b><br /><br />Thank you for the buddy read <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1470105103" rel="nofollow noopener">Aileene</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1563942667" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a> :D</span>

        rated it

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4150124-aileene?shelf=buddy-read">buddy-read</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1470105103" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15714374640459287696">Licking this muscles clean with my lovelies <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-nynaeve' rel='nofollow noopener'>Jess</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp' rel='nofollow noopener'>Alp</a> tomorrow, 29 Feb<br/><br/>Yup. Abundance of muscles indeed but the story? Eh.<br/><br/>I give points to the mountain of muscles on the cover *mouths* but I hated the pose - it didn't do any good to me.<br/><br/>The other point goes out to our heroine, Becca. She was courageous and had stayed positive during the first bit of their captivity. I like those traits in my heroines. I'm not a man but I get a raging hard on when female roles display characters such as this.<br/><br/>So </span>
  <span id="freeText15714374640459287696" style="display:none">Licking this muscles clean with my lovelies <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/27279812-jess-j-rex-the-book-eating-dinosaur-nynaeve" rel="nofollow noopener">Jess</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/26653561-alp" rel="nofollow noopener">Alp</a> tomorrow, 29 Feb<br><br>Yup. Abundance of muscles indeed but the story? Eh.<br><br>I give points to the mountain of muscles on the cover *mouths* but I hated the pose - it didn't do any good to me.<br><br>The other point goes out to our heroine, Becca. She was courageous and had stayed positive during the first bit of their captivity. I like those traits in my heroines. I'm not a man but I get a raging hard on when female roles display characters such as this.<br><br>So for these two, I give this.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457308733ra/18345090.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But.<br><br>Yes, there's a but because these were short lived. Becca turned into a nightmare after few pages in. <br><br>Ok. <br>This is the fifth installment of NS. We have Brawn and Becca this time.<br>Brawn who was introduced at the last part of Valiant's book. <br>Becca on the other hand was a military brat. Her dad was Tim Oberto, Jessie Dupree's old boss.<br><br>They met. There was an attraction. And then they were captured and caged.<br>Caged. <br>Brawn was locked in a cage for so long, getting maltreated and experimented. So, it was only fitting that I expected fear, rage and non stop violence from him but it didn't happen. <br>What he and Becca did was they bonked. <br>They banged. <br>They copped a root. <br>How would one feel if one was recaptured and was put back in a cage again? Surely, not have hot sexes. Right? Right.<br>Whilst the executed sexy times were hot, I couldn't get myself to like it. It was wrong and was misplaced.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457308733i/18345091.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Another thing, all characters are plain stupid ESP the hero and heroine. <br>People, assuming things won't help. F*kn talk to each other.<br>The story dragged because of this.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457308733i/18345092.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, why does everyone have the need to dip in and meddle in everyone's relationships? Steer clear and get the f*ck off and let the ones IN the relationship to talk and sort things out themselves.<br>They're consenting adults and do not need anyone's interference.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457308733i/18345093.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh and what was all the misleading information of medication about?<br>Whatever universe you're in, you can't just give medication to anybody without informing the recipient what it was for. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457308733i/18345094.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> for whatever reason you may have, it is unacceptable. <br>And no matter what angle you look at it, it is f*kn wrong. That is taking away one's decision. <br><br>And lastly, Tim Oberto who was a dick and cannot see reasons became a big teddy bear all of a sudden at the end? So wrong and did not fit rightly in with his character.<br><br>The book held a promise at the start and ended poorly and leaving me wanting to do this<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457308733i/18345095._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Rating this <b>1.5</b> <i>Taking-a-breather-from-this-series</i> <b>Stars</b></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17595253243239533263">Okay. . . Confession. . . Laurann is my crit-partner so I've read this book (don't hate me) and I have to tell you. . .   <span id="freeText17595253243239533263" style="display:none">Okay. . . Confession. . . Laurann is my crit-partner so I've read this book (don't hate me) and I have to tell you. . . I was nervous going into this one. . . Justice was such a powerhouse book. There'd been a big build up to the leader of the New Species book and amazingly Justice's book was one of those that actually lived up to the hype. I think Justice was better than we all expected and that was saying something!!<br /><br />So with Brawn I was wringing my hands because I thought. . . How can she possibly top the awesomeness of Justice?<br /><br />Well. . . Let me tell you. . . She did it! I stayed up ALL NIGHT to finish Brawn. She completely sucked me in with Brawn and Becca's story. . . And you have to consider me having a baby and two other children. Staying up all night to finish pre-reading a story I could have easily waited until morning to finish was madness. . . but that's how incredible this story is!! It's still with me and I read it a while ago!<br /><br />Be excited about the upcoming release. . . On Dec. 27 BUY BRAWN!!! You will love it!! This series gets better and better and better and I'm so thankful Laurann created this wonderful world we all get to visit and fall in love with! <br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17754471839743241835">I think this might just be my favorite in this series so far! I REALLY loved Brawn...and i loved how protective he was of Becca when they were held captive. I also actually liked Becca. After reading some reviews i was expecting her to be extremely un-likeable (i really need to stop reading reviews before i read a book, especially when the book hasn't been rated so well...not that people don't have a right to their opinions if they've disliked something...i just think when there are negative com</span>
  <span id="freeText17754471839743241835" style="display:none">I think this might just be my favorite in this series so far! I REALLY loved Brawn...and i loved how protective he was of Becca when they were held captive. I also actually liked Becca. After reading some reviews i was expecting her to be extremely un-likeable (i really need to stop reading reviews before i read a book, especially when the book hasn't been rated so well...not that people don't have a right to their opinions if they've disliked something...i just think when there are negative comments made i go in with reservations and i keep anticipating the "bad stuff!" LOL!). I thought Becca handled their captivity really well and was rather sweet with Brawn in there. The only time that she frustrated me was when she was so upset that she wouldn't allow Brawn to explain himself...i felt really sorry for him :( ...then again...she was sort of justified in thinking he only wanted her back for one reason..<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[that she was pregnant...he didn't contact her for over two months though!...why wouldn't she think the worse? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> ..it's just unfortunate that her father manipulated the whole thing making them BOTH think that neither of them wanted anything to do w/ the other after everything that had happened to them. Although Brawn going all "he-man" on Becca when she returned didn't exactly help the "situation" either..good thing he had Trisha and Breeze to help explain things to Becca! After reading the entire book i can see how some might dislike Becca for how she treated Brawn but again...WE knew the "real story" but she did not and sadly she was just trying to protect herself from a repeat of her last marriage. <br /><br />All in all, i thoroughly enjoyed this book..more than i thought i would! I do wish Tiger's book was next..another character i've really enjoyed in all the books! Wrath is apparently who the next book is about and i can honestly say i have NO CLUE who that is...but here's hoping it will be as entertaining as the rest have been! :)</span>

              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16046484877453319612">I totally enjoyed this book. I liked the way that Brawn was so gentle with her and protective of her. I liked the outgoing say anything heroine. I continue to really enjoy this series. The men are just always so sweet. I've read some reviews that said the stories are really similar to each other plot wise but I don't care at all. In fact I like it. I like stories where the man is some paranormal something and the woman is human and the book is about them meeting and her learning to deal with his</span>
  <span id="freeText16046484877453319612" style="display:none">I totally enjoyed this book. I liked the way that Brawn was so gentle with her and protective of her. I liked the outgoing say anything heroine. I continue to really enjoy this series. The men are just always so sweet. I've read some reviews that said the stories are really similar to each other plot wise but I don't care at all. In fact I like it. I like stories where the man is some paranormal something and the woman is human and the book is about them meeting and her learning to deal with his otherness and him learning to love a human woman. It's a formula that works for me and I'll keep signing up to read it. I don't need any huge overarching story that begins to take over the falling in love aspect that happens in many paranormal series. I don't mind a continuing thread or two but I'm reading for the love story. That is well done in this series so far.<br /><br />The plot here made sense. There was sweet romance, some heated sex and some angst. Good book.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1292175841058943038">I enjoyed this book. The series has, for the most part, been very good (I’m still going to pretend Valiant doesn’t exist). <br/><br/>I don’t have any complaints about the book but one thing did bother me. When Jessie and Justice were talking to Becca’s father, I felt like they were talking to him like he was a kid. I know they were worried that he would try to attack or kill Brawn, but come on!   <span id="freeText1292175841058943038" style="display:none">I enjoyed this book. The series has, for the most part, been very good (I’m still going to pretend Valiant doesn’t exist). <br /><br />I don’t have any complaints about the book but one thing did bother me. When Jessie and Justice were talking to Becca’s father, I felt like they were talking to him like he was a kid. I know they were worried that he would try to attack or kill Brawn, but come on! Give the guy some credit. Don’t they know the difference between venting in anger and actions?<br /><br />I really liked Brawn and Becca together, and they had to deal with some rough situations. I think one of my favorite moments was right after Becca was brought to Reservation <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[when Becca was being transferred from the Clinic to the Hotel. When Brawn was on his knees asking her not to send him away. That was the first time in the books where the hero has really opened himself and his emotions up to the heroine before the end of the book <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>. Brawn rivals Slade for my favorite New Species, pushing Justice back to the second position. <br /><br />I’m really looking forward to reading the next book in the series. <br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722516312" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer18114092802637080544">4 stars<br/><br/>This was a very good story. I liked both Becca and Brawn and enjoyed their story. I'm really liking this series and am planning to continue with it.<br/><br/>Becca is the daughter of Tim, the leader of the human task force that works with the NSO (the New Species Organization). She's a widow and lives alone in a house that she inherited from her grandfather, which happens to be on the same land as her Father's house. When Tim has a NS male coming to stay with him as a new member of the team, Tim tr</span>
  <span id="freeText18114092802637080544" style="display:none">4 stars<br /><br />This was a very good story. I liked both Becca and Brawn and enjoyed their story. I'm really liking this series and am planning to continue with it.<br /><br />Becca is the daughter of Tim, the leader of the human task force that works with the NSO (the New Species Organization). She's a widow and lives alone in a house that she inherited from her grandfather, which happens to be on the same land as her Father's house. When Tim has a NS male coming to stay with him as a new member of the team, Tim tries to give him Becca's house (telling her to move in with him) but Becca's not about to be chased out of her house or let her Father order her around. As a result, she stays in her house but lets the NS male, Brawn, stay in her guest bedroom.<br /><br />Brawn is a member of the NS council and agreed to help out the human task force that's been working on retrieving NS people that are still captives in secret labs and such. When he arrived at the place he's to stay, he finds himself confronted with a small, human female that he's strongly attracted to, regardless of the fact that he never thought he'd want a human female (thinking they're too delicate and soft). He resolves to try to do his job without giving in to temptation.<br /><br />Brawn and Becca have issues almost immediately. The first night Brawn spends in Becca's house, they're attacked by a team of men that manage to drug Brawn and take them both captive. They take Becca because they believe she's his girlfriend and want to use her to control him and for some procedures they're doing. While they're held captive, Brawn and Becca both start to have deeper feelings for each other. They become closer and even come together once during their captivity. They both want more with the other and worries that the way they're being held captive might cause problems for them being together later. Unfortunately, they don't get much of a chance to talk things out as every time either Becca or Brawn seems about to say something helpful, they get interrupted. Becca and Brawn end up rescued before they've worked things out between them and a well-meaning but rather assholish intervention ends up keeping them apart after the rescue.<br /><br />Becca and Brawn both end up heart-broken and thinking the other doesn't want them. Brawn tries to live his life. Becca goes off to hide in a cabin and get away from everyone due to an unforeseen circumstance that comes from her and Brawn's time together. Despite her reasons for hiding, she ends up at the Reserve (and NSO compound) against her will but for her own safety. Brawn finds out she's there and goes after her but Becca thinks he's only there because he feels guilty and not because he wants her. They end up going through some tough times as she believes he really wants an NS female and Brawn doesn't understand what is wrong and how to convince her to be with him. I guess when you grow up in a lab, relationship skills and understanding women aren't things you learn...poor Brawn. LOL. With a little help from some new friends, Becca does end up convinced of Brawn's feelings and agrees to be with him and they get a sweet HEA.<br /><br />This was a very good story. I really liked Brawn and Becca and was so frustrated as they were trying to get past their mis-conceptions and issues, so I was very happy to see them work things out. I can't wait to read the next book in the series. I'd recommend this book. Thumbs up! :D<br /><br />* note - I listened to the audio version of this book. The narrator did a pretty good job.</span>
  <a data-text-id="18114092802637080544" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1223193891" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1223193891" />
    <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--"><img alt="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1555353893p2/3161105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1223193891?book_show_action=true">Mar 09, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»" href="/user/show/3161105-maida---v--">Maida»-(¯`v´¯)-»</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3161105-maida---v--?shelf=erotica">erotica</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1223193891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9127275351605510580"><br/><b>RATING: 3 "Much Better" Hearts</b><br/><br/><i>Brawn</i> is the fifth addition to the <u>New Species</u> series, and fortunately for my sake, it was an enjoyable step-up from the colossal mess that was <i>Justice</i>. That's not to say, it didn't have flaws – it did – but the flaws are more of an annoying background noise in face of the moderately fun storyline, and pleasing characters.<br/><br/>This series has a serious tendency to overlap with its plot, but, surprisingly, this one was different, in that it takes us right to the core of t</span>
  <span id="freeText9127275351605510580" style="display:none"><br /><b>RATING: 3 "Much Better" Hearts</b><br /><br /><i>Brawn</i> is the fifth addition to the <u>New Species</u> series, and fortunately for my sake, it was an enjoyable step-up from the colossal mess that was <i>Justice</i>. That's not to say, it didn't have flaws – it did – but the flaws are more of an annoying background noise in face of the moderately fun storyline, and pleasing characters.<br /><br />This series has a serious tendency to overlap with its plot, but, surprisingly, this one was different, in that it takes us right to the core of the bad guys' den. Majority of the story is spent with Brawn and Becca after they get captured, and it was nice to learn the big picture behind Mercile, the bad guys who created New Species, instead of being stuck at Homeland or Reservation. This story takes us into the human world, and every plot revelation is interesting, and not in the least bit dull. <br /><br />Along with the engaging plot, both the main characters are a nice reprieve from the usual characters with their million and one reasons why they can't be together. Brawn is badass, intense and sweet, whereas, Becca is strong, brave, and also badass in her own way. Both of them are perfect for one another with their similar yet contrasting personalities, making them a couple whose story I could easily get behind, and actually find memorable. The smexy scenes are ever raunchy, but in this I found a sweet romance as well. It's not all about the lust, and somewhere along the way, emotions come into play, making us feel the love Brawn and Becca share.<br /><br />Although, this could have gone without the <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[unnecessary baby drama that ensues near the end and the <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> lack of communication. All it takes is a few words to clear up a HUGE situation, but it doesn't get done until the very last possible second. Cliche, and beyond burdensome and annoying. So, no major reasons why they can't be together, but communication problems galore. I suspect, this is one aspect in the eroitca genre that will <b>never</b> change.<br /><br />Overall, I enjoyed the story and the characters, and aside from the reservations I had, Laurann Dohner did good with this. Looking forward to what the next book, <u>Wrath</u>, has to offer.<br /><br /><br /><br /><b>
  <i>Posted: March 30, 2015</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="9127275351605510580" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lynsey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lynsey" href="/user/show/2985074-lynsey">Lynsey</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2985074-lynsey?shelf=romance-paranormal">romance-paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer239510137&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer239510137" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10519767471349899802">Listened to on audio. Narrated by Vanessa Chambers.<br/><br/>I really enjoyed this one, but I must add that it really *really* pushed my buttons at times!<br/><br/>I liked both Brawn and Becca. <br/><br/>Becca doesn't seem to have been very popular with people and I don't think I really understand why. I thought she was really likeable, but I don't understand people who are pushed around by their family. I kept willing her to tell her Dad where to stick it and I was a little disappointed that we never saw her confront him ab</span>
  <span id="freeText10519767471349899802" style="display:none">Listened to on audio. Narrated by Vanessa Chambers.<br /><br />I really enjoyed this one, but I must add that it really *really* pushed my buttons at times!<br /><br />I liked both Brawn and Becca. <br /><br />Becca doesn't seem to have been very popular with people and I don't think I really understand why. I thought she was really likeable, but I don't understand people who are pushed around by their family. I kept willing her to tell her Dad where to stick it and I was a little disappointed that we never saw her confront him about his unreasonable behaviour. I-do-it-because-I-love-you is a pathetic excuse for being so controlling and disrespectful to her. <br /><br />Despite that, I had a lot of admiration for her. I found it hard to listen as people over and over again betrayed her trust. Brawn (when she thought he didn't want her), her Dad, her dead husband, Tricia, Brawn again (when she thought he was seeing other women). I was actually impressed by her strength. Even when it seemed the whole world was betraying her, she pulled up her big girl panties and got on with it. I'd have shot Brawn in the man-parts if that was me. Yes yes, I know he hadn't actually done anything, but that is beside the point! She thought he had.<br /><br />Now, Brawn I loved. He was the usual dominating demanding sex god that we all enjoy from this writer. I never get bored of that guy! I felt sorry for Brawn when Becca kept pushing him away and I liked that he never gave up. I know other people found Becca frustrating for this, however, for me I totally understood where she was coming from and she was hurting. I thought Becca was pretty dignified under stress (apart from when she eats or drinks alcohol - that was really not classy!).<br /><br />One bizarre thing was Tricia and her abso-f*ckin-lutely unacceptable behaviour giving Becca pills to unknowingly abort her baby. What the heck?<br /><br />Despite that strange wtf moment, I absolutely loved this one!</span>
  <a data-text-id="10519767471349899802" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17370374170848059495">First, the positive:<br/>- A fresher plot. Not fresh, definitely not unique, but at least mostly different from the other 4 books.<br/>-Less sex, more action (it is good even if you're a smutty reader :D, the scenes were copy carbon. You'll understand when reading).<br/><br/>The negative:<br/>-Flat characterization. Well, Ms Dohner's character are never that well written, but let's say this bunch is flatter than usual and "choppier" too. <br/>The way Tim behaved is difficult to believe (and keep his job and other people's tr</span>
  <span id="freeText17370374170848059495" style="display:none">First, the positive:<br />- A fresher plot. Not fresh, definitely not unique, but at least mostly different from the other 4 books.<br />-Less sex, more action (it is good even if you're a smutty reader :D, the scenes were copy carbon. You'll understand when reading).<br /><br />The negative:<br />-Flat characterization. Well, Ms Dohner's character are never that well written, but let's say this bunch is flatter than usual and "choppier" too. <br />The way Tim behaved is difficult to believe (and keep his job and other people's trust) and totally unacceptable. This made the HEA unbelievable.<br />-Some repetition got really boring for me. His fear, her fear. Same and again.<br />-A weak heroine, fearful and unable to stand up for herself. <br /><br />For those of us who are playing this game: <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/1707240.Aiden_s_Charity__Breeds___12_" title="Aiden's Charity (Breeds, #12) by Lora Leigh" rel="nofollow noopener">Aiden's Charity</a>, without her strength and intelligence. <br /><br />Last, but not least, please EC do something about covers. They are getting worse (and were never that good to begin with). <br /><br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6266483175544350043">4.5 Brawn Stars <br/><br/>Being as this is a reread I already knew I would enjoy the book. But I was surprised at how much I liked Brawn. I never gave his character a second thought from the other books. <br/><br/>Tim O’bearto I did though, I thought dang that guy needs to get laid. Hahaha so when you find out it's his daughter who Brawn falls for you know it’s going to be a damn fine book, to say the least. <br/><br/>I love Becca’s spunk, and how she doesn't back down.   <span id="freeText6266483175544350043" style="display:none">4.5 Brawn Stars <br /><br />Being as this is a reread I already knew I would enjoy the book. But I was surprised at how much I liked Brawn. I never gave his character a second thought from the other books. <br /><br />Tim O’bearto I did though, I thought dang that guy needs to get laid. Hahaha so when you find out it's his daughter who Brawn falls for you know it’s going to be a damn fine book, to say the least. <br /><br />I love Becca’s spunk, and how she doesn't back down. I love that she also feels so much but there is one thing I am not a fan of from her and that is how much she protested. I get why and all but it was a little annoying. But thank goodness for Brawn he showed her the way. Hahhahaha <br /><br />Again I am a fan of the narrator! Vanessa does a freaking fantastic job with these characters…love, love, love.<br /><br />*You don't have to like my review but its 100% my opinion, and I am allowed to have it.*</span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7B3U/9ILqwtBiEqtpwC61w2lErRQ0mAWoVX0b+/ICz1iSrnQnb/FIHw6jl532iHOGlTrlvVdOn02iFCEiVgrNg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('um0mPC1zqaiuJwNoqaHqA126U3wfj+ITI7OZmxL7PTc0OksTYsfHg5OVx5t5e3EaSkuqXroAuHi0bj1wdGsdPA==')})
  }

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer1931448993946000070">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've alw</span>
  <span id="freeText1931448993946000070" style="display:none">I had a rather short area here telling a little about me but then I had more than a few people ask me to expand it so... here goes. LOL. I'm a full time home 'supervisor' which is a nice word for saying I'm a housewife. I'm married happily, I met my dream guy 20 years ago, and we have 4 children. I live in Southern California and I can't function without iced coffee. I believe in romance, I've always been a daydreamer, and I'm a HUGE fan of books, always have been.<br /><br />No, I didn't know that I always wanted to write. I inhaled books as a child. I read entire series (Pippi Longstocking, Nancy Drew and The Hardy Boys, Trixie Beldon, The Borrowers, etc) in a matter of days at a time. By the time I was nine years old I had an adult library card where I visited often. I moved on to John Saul, Stephen King, Richard Laymon, Agatha Christie, and then found romance. I was hooked. I wrote poetry in my teens and then moved on to short stories. My first book was started after I read a real bomb of a book that ticked me off with really horrible characters and a plot that was shabby at best and I thought... I could do better. LOL.<br /><br />I wrote my first book which will probably never see the light of day in the early 90's. I wrote a series of a few books from it. I'm a series fan! I kept writing for fun, wrote MANY books and then in 2009 I decided to try to get published. I wrote my first Sci Fi romance and Ral's Woman came to be. I submitted it and with a little tweaking, Ellorascave sent me an acceptance letter. It was kind of a 'Cinderella' experience for me. It's been a terrific ride so far and I'm really happy that I finally had the time to commit to writing full time. It's a dream come true.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1931448993946000070" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });
        });
      $('bookCover_17987085').observe('prototip:hidden', function () {
        $$('span.elementTwo').each(function (e) {
          if (e.getStyle('display') !== 'none') {
            var lessLink = e.next();
            swapContent(lessLink);
          }
        });
      });

//]]>
</script>

</li>
</ul>
</div>
